  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f0fd34ff-a270-47ec-8c77-b46432bd6ceb'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <b>A USA Today Bestseller about reclaiming the love of a lifetime...</b>

  <span id="freeText17457263754513606855" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>A USA Today Bestseller about reclaiming the love of a lifetime...</b>
</i><br /><br />Growing up in an idealistic home, Sparrow Fisher is sheltered and innocent. When she meets Ian Sterling, a musician who is rising in popularity, she instantly falls for his charm. The attraction is instant, but their relationship isn't so simple.<br /><br />At different places in their lives, Sparrow is off to college in New York, and Ian is traveling the country with the band. Over a five year span, Sparrow and Ian run into each other in unusual places. Each time, Sparrow has to decide if she can trust him, and if he feels the same for her. It’s hard to not get caught up in the magic they have together. <br /><br />Until something so devastating comes to light that threatens to shatter everything they’ve built with each other.<br /><br />True Love Story is a story about the real highs and lows that come with a relationship—happiness, pain, angst, and finding out if love really is enough.</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/209785-i-wish-there-was-a-book-from-ian-s-pov-or">I wish there was a book from Ian&#39;s POV. Or maybe a couple chapters from his POV. That would have made the book perfect. It&#39;s so hard to understand what he did. I wish there was more about his relationship with Laila to really understand his decisions. Does anyone else feel this way?</a>
</div>

<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/25085514-mary"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1383060240i/25085514._UY100_CR39,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/25085514-mary">Mary</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I wish there were more with these characters as well, but I think what happened with Laila was very simple. She wanted him, and she threw herself at h<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I wish there were more with these characters as well, but I think what happened with Laila was very simple. She wanted him, and she threw herself at him. When he resisted, she brought up things that played upon his insecurities. Ian is a very needy person to be in a long-distance relationship successfully and has too much baggage from his childhood to really feel good about himself and secure. He didn't love himself, so he engaged in self-sabotaging behavior. Ian is very similar to Kellan Kyle (from SC Stephens' Thoughtless series) in personality and motivations. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10506048758766472675"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509005066i/24275821._SX540_.jpg' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508425345ra/24212327.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508821482ra/24257700.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508821482ra/24257701.gif' width='420' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️! True <s>Love</s> Story (stand-alone). Student is swept off her feet by older musician. A whirlwind affair wreaked by lies & betrayal!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“The evening feels like a long love letter, with sweet touches and looks speaking volumes of truth.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>True <s>Love</s> Story</b> opens up two years ten months after an ended relationship. Story then skips back half a decade in time to when eighteen year old <b>Sparrow Fisher, Rosie aka Little Bird</b> meets twenty-seven year old up-and-coming musician <b>Ian </b></span>
  <span id="freeText10506048758766472675" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1509005066i/24275821._SX540_.jpg" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508425345ra/24212327.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508821482ra/24257700.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508821482ra/24257701.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️! True <s>Love</s> Story (stand-alone). Student is swept off her feet by older musician. A whirlwind affair wreaked by lies &amp; betrayal!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“The evening feels like a long love letter, with sweet touches and looks speaking volumes of truth.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>True <s>Love</s> Story</b> opens up two years ten months after an ended relationship. Story then skips back half a decade in time to when eighteen year old <b>Sparrow Fisher, Rosie aka Little Bird</b> meets twenty-seven year old up-and-coming musician <b>Ian Sterling.</b><br><br>And so an easy hot-cold flirtation begins. Sparrow is in over her head with the charming, slippery and aloof Ian yet she has something that captivates him and has him coming back for more.<br><br>Follow them in their <b>doomed love.</b> You know it is going to end, you know it’s going to be painful. (it includes cheating!) It’s like waiting for the other shoe to drop, but when it does it still hurts like the motherload.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509003264ra/24275701.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Five words to describe <b> Ian Orville Sterling:</b> Charismatic, aloof, complex, enigmatic and unpredictable.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509001822ra/24275551.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Five words to describe <b> Sparrow Kate Fisher, Rosie aka Little Bird:</b> Reflective, naïve, confident, trusting and patient.<br><br><b>True <s>Love</s> Story,</b> told from dual POVs will hurt in the best possible way. An <b>all-consuming</b> love starting as a slow-burning, sweet, and beyond sexy romance only to intensify before raging out-of-control into heart-wrenching betrayal. Go in blind and just feel it!<br><br>***<br>Hero: ★★★★1/2<br>Heroine: ★★★★1/2<br>Plot: ★★★★★<br>Storytelling: ★★★★★<br>Sexual tension: ★★★★★<br>Sex scenes: ★★★★1/2<br>Story ending: ★★★★1/2<br>******************************************<br><b>OVERALL RATING:</b> ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Angst: <b>| HIGH FOCUS |</b><br>Darkness: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Humor: <b>| LOW FOCUS |</b><br>Kink: <b>| LOW FOCUS |</b><br>Romance: <b>| HIGH FOCUS |</b><br>Sex frequency: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br>Suspense: <b>| MEDIUM FOCUS |</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508822271ra/24257770.gif" width="420" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10506048758766472675" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_485754019" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/485754019" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/485754019?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485754019" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7710410358661218762"><br/><b>**4.5 HEART<s>BREAKING</s>WARMING STARS!!!!**</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402081i/781294.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Love is enough.<br/>Love does conquer all.<br/>Love really does always protect, trust, hope, persevere...<br/>I'd even go as far as saying that love never fails. I finally believe that."</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/><b>True <s>Love</s> Story</b> is indeed a story about <b>
  <i>true love</i>
</b>. It's a story about the kind of love that lasts a lifetime but that is faced with so many obstacles and bumps along the way that sometimes the ones in love begin to wonder if love itself is enough. They begin to wonder if their love</span>
  <span id="freeText7710410358661218762" style="display:none"><br><b>**4.5 HEART<s>BREAKING</s>WARMING STARS!!!!**</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402081i/781294.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Love is enough.<br>Love does conquer all.<br>Love really does always protect, trust, hope, persevere...<br>I'd even go as far as saying that love never fails. I finally believe that."</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>True <s>Love</s> Story</b> is indeed a story about <b>
  <i>true love</i>
</b>. It's a story about the kind of love that lasts a lifetime but that is faced with so many obstacles and bumps along the way that sometimes the ones in love begin to wonder if love itself is enough. They begin to wonder if their love is really worth holding onto and fighting for... <br><br><br><b>Sparrow Fisher --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402081i/781295._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story starts off in the present when the 24 year old Sparrow Fisher bumps into her ex, Ian Sterling at the airport. They were once madly in love but somehow Ian managed to break Sparrow's heart in the most cruel way possible and now it's been a long time since she's last seen him...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It's been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him. Two years, ten months, and five days since he broke my heart - well, since I knew that he had broken my heart. <br><br>Technically, he began breaking my heart the moment I met him, five years, eleven months and one day ago."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>After that, the story shift back to the past and we learn all about how Ian and Sparrow first met and how their entire relationship slowly grew into something more than either of them could have ever expected.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"All my life I've said what everyone wanted me to say, worn what everyone wanted me to wear, acted just so - never realizing until this very moment that I've been waiting for someone to look past it all and actually see <u>me</u>." ~ Sparrow</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Ian Sterling --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402081i/781296._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>A musician with a tortured soul.<br><br>A heartbreaker, a womanizer, but also a lover and a fighter.</i>
</b><br><br>Together they are <b>perfect</b> for each other. He's the older, more experienced one. She's the pure soul, full of life and she manages to bring out a caring side of him that he's never been able to show before. They have fun, they laugh but they also know that relationships aren't always easy. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're going to break my heart, Sparrow Fisher." And I think, Not before you break mine.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Although their relationship wasn't always easy (with Ian being on tour a lot so sometimes they didn't see each other for months), I loved how playful they were together and how they were always able to completely be their selves around each other.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Well, my number is the same. I will never change it. You know, hoping one day you'll call and say you're taking me back," he says earnestly. <br><br>~~<br><br>"You're impossible."<br>"You're delectable."<br>"You're incorrigible."<br>"You're edible."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402081i/781297.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You are my first<br>And last<br>And only<br>True Love --"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402081i/781298.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Little Bird, our love has been hard-earned from the very beginning. It is more precious to me than anything on earth. I can't just let go of it. And I won't stop fighting for it." ~ Ian</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><br>Around 77% into the story something happened that left me speechless and thinking-<p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402081ra/781299.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p>Admittedly, I did see it coming somehow, but still, it broke my heart and made me furious for a while. Especially the last 30 % of the story were highly emotional and I kept feeling very anxious to find out how it was going to end. And well, I can't tell you exactly how it ends only that is does have a <b>HEA</b>.☺<br><br>I laughed, I cried, then I laughed and cried some more... It was a heartbreaking story that managed to grasp my attention from the moment I started reading it. I really loved how the author managed to describe all the emotions Sparrow went through, so well. It was an interesting process to see her change from a young, insecure girl into a well developed grown woman who knew exactly what she wanted. I absolutely loved reading the story from Sparrow's point of view, she's a very easy-to-relate-with character and some of her inner monologues literally made me laugh out loud. I think the author <b>Willow Aster</b> did a wonderful job at describing this realistic story about love and everything that comes with it.<br><br>To everyone who hasn't read this beautiful, captivating story yet, I would say <b>
  <u>READ IT</u>
</b>, give it a try and hopefully you'll enjoy it just as much as I did!!!!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402081i/781300.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****<br><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"When I got home, I took out my journal titled Important Things that Happened in my 14th Year and wrote: I Saw Ian Sterling. I've been looking for him ever since."<br><br>~~~<br><br>"He asked me out a half dozen times before I said yes. If he'd just shown me his chest, we could have settled the matter much sooner."<br><br>~~~<br><br>"Never hesitate to tell the truth. It's the only way it will be any good."<br><br>~~~<br><br>"I've been looking for you, his eyes are saying.<br>You've found me now, I'm certain my eyes are saying."<br><br>~~~<br><br>"All kisses before this have been mere child's play. I drink him in and know my fate is sealed: I am his."<br><br><br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br>****<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7710410358661218762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_560880783" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/560880783" />
    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/560880783?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dd" href="/user/show/9444787-dd">Dd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer560880783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14584531337803681895"><br/><b>Hello Readers!!</b><br/><br/>Let me tell you about a story!<br/><br/>There was this girl....young, beautiful and full of life.<br/><br/>And then one day she meets with the man of her dreams.<br/><br/>And they live happily ever after.....<br/><br/><b>Or do they???</b><br/><br/><i>"It has been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him.Two years, ten months and five days since he broke my heart.Technically, he began breaking my heart the moment I met him, five years, eleven months, and one day ago."</i><br/><br/>-------------------------------------------------------</span>
  <span id="freeText14584531337803681895" style="display:none"><br /><b>Hello Readers!!</b><br /><br />Let me tell you about a story!<br /><br />There was this girl....young, beautiful and full of life.<br /><br />And then one day she meets with the man of her dreams.<br /><br />And they live happily ever after.....<br /><br /><b>Or do they???</b><br /><br /><i>"It has been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him.Two years, ten months and five days since he broke my heart.Technically, he began breaking my heart the moment I met him, five years, eleven months, and one day ago."</i><br /><br />------------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>Five years, eleven months, and one day ago....</b><br /><br />Sparrow is transforming.From a girl into a woman.Finally unleashing her wilder side.<br /><br />And it is then she meets with the man whose songs had touched her, owned her, and claimed her at a concert four years ago.<br /><br /><br />Ian Sterling.<br /><br /><br /><b>And then....something happens, something shifts, something clicks.</b><br /><br />And the funny thing is that....she doesn't even believe in love at first sight.<br /><br /><br /><i>"I've been looking for you,his eyes are saying.<br />You've found me now,I'm certain my eyes are responding."</i><br /><br /><br />It all starts then.Five years, eleven months, and one day ago.<br /><br />This story of Ian and Sparrow.<br /><br />Their <b>
  <s>LOVE</s>
</b> story.<br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Okay Readers...I just don't know how to rate this book.I did not even like it for most of the parts.But I thoroughly enjoyed a few.<br /><br />For a long time I could not get the point of this story.<br /><br />At times I hated both Ian and Sparrow.<br /><br /><b>But somewhere, somehow, this struck a chord within me.</b> <br /><br />I don't know how,just that it did.And even though this book contains what I consider a <b>deal breaker</b>,the feeling remains.<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"You're going to break my heart, Sparrow Fisher." And I think, Not before you break mine.</i>
</b><br /><br />Over the course of five years,they meet over and over again.And every time,they fall more and more in love.<br /><br />Sometimes it was sweet, sometimes maddening, sometimes irritating and sometimes lovely.<br /><br />Sometimes I wanted to shake some sense into them.<br /><br />And then came the climax....God, I hated it.<br /><br /><i>How could he do that? Why did he do that?</i><br /><br />God damn it.<br /><br /><br />So yes,I too was compelled to ask the question....<br /><br /><br /><b>IS LOVE REALLY ENOUGH?</b><br /><br /><i>To forgive as well as forget?</i><br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><br />That's all for now,Readers.<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!<br /><br /><br />P.S. -<b>
  <i> “Love is enough.<br />Love does conquer all.<br />Love really does always protect, trust, hope, persevere...<br />I'd even go as far as saying that love never fails. I finally believe that.” </i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer484822728" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12011060023435125697"><b>MINOR SPOILERS in a section marked<u> minor spoilers</u>-you've been warned</b> <br/>-mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>4 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: New Adult Romance<br/><br/>This...wait...excuse me.<br/>*Inhales slowly, exhales slowly*<br/>This is one of those books you finish and think<br/><br/><a href='http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_lq12l1XdZO1qdqf97o1_500_zps45a98163.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>At the end I could not believe how strongly this<b> Heart-breaking-Earth-shattering</b> <i>love</i> story resonated with me. But..it did.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/emotional%20words%20gifs/tumblr_mi2wx94wiL1r3gi71o1_500_zps2b91bd88.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380315268ra/688983.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mi2wx94wiL1r3gi71o1_500_zps2b91bd88.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Please please bare with me I have so much to say and all of my thoughts are hitting me at once.<br/>Honestly this is </span>
  <span id="freeText12011060023435125697" style="display:none"><b>MINOR SPOILERS in a section marked<u> minor spoilers</u>-you've been warned</b> <br>-mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><br>This...wait...excuse me.<br>*Inhales slowly, exhales slowly*<br>This is one of those books you finish and think<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_lq12l1XdZO1qdqf97o1_500_zps45a98163.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401940ra/780721.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lq12l1XdZO1qdqf97o1_500_zps45a98163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>At the end I could not believe how strongly this<b> Heart-breaking-Earth-shattering</b> <i>love</i> story resonated with me. But..it did.<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/emotional%20words%20gifs/tumblr_mi2wx94wiL1r3gi71o1_500_zps2b91bd88.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380315268ra/688983.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mi2wx94wiL1r3gi71o1_500_zps2b91bd88.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Please please bare with me I have so much to say and all of my thoughts are hitting me at once.<br>Honestly this is the closest I have come to giving a book 5 stars in 2013... It did something to me.. The authors style lit up my taste buds perfectly... Her way with words... The story itself... The characters, oh dear lord the characters are embedded in my brain. I laughed, I cried both tears of joy and tears of sorrow. More importantly I learned from this book that LOVE heals even the deepest of wounds. The ones so deep you think it will never close, the ones that make you feel as if your at deaths door because the pain is unbearable. <br><b> 'He reaches over and grabs my hand and laces our fingers together.</b> <i>
  <b> “You’re going to break my heart, Sparrow Fisher.” </b>
</i> <b> And I think, Not before you break mine.'</b><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_lp377soVhE1qm19vto1_500_zps6f8c0bcd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400460ra/776060.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lp377soVhE1qm19vto1_500_zps6f8c0bcd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>When the book starts we meet Sparrow and immediately learn that she has been dealing with a broken heart.<br><i>
  <b> 'It has been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him. Two years, ten months, and five days since he broke my heart—well, since I knew that he had broken my heart. Technically, he began breaking my heart the moment I met him, five years, eleven months, and one day ago.'</b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/tears%20tears%20and%20more%20tears/crying_zps56e23308.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401940ra/780722.gif" alt=" photo crying_zps56e23308.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b> 'I’ve got a hundred kisses for every tear I’ve caused. A hug for every heartache. Oh, I miss you. My body aches.<br>My heart groans. I call your name and hope that somewhere deep in your spirit, you’ll hear… I love you. Ian'</b>
</i><br><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/5b67beda-2668-4fb5-a1d6-9809889c4b87_zpse6ac4beb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401940i/780723.jpg" alt=" photo 5b67beda-2668-4fb5-a1d6-9809889c4b87_zpse6ac4beb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Sparrow Fisher is the daughter of a preacher. She wears what she is told to wear and says what she is suppose to say. A true all around good girl with her virtue still in tact. Soon all of her good girl wardrobe will be put to pasture; she recently graduated high school and will be leaving her California roots to move clear across the country and attend NYU. She's been in a comfortable 4 month relationship with Michael the youth pastor at her fathers church. She's grounded her future looks good from the view she sees.. Sparrow has no idea that her world is about to be lifted off its axis the second she meets Ian Sterling.<br><br><br>**Whispers**<b>Guess who's coming to dinner....</b><br>Sparrow attends a planned dinner with her boyfriend, her parents and family friends; a couple by the name of Jeff and Laila. When she enters the restaurant she recognizes him immediately and alerts her mother of his presence. Ian Sterling. A singer, song writer and musician. Introductions are made and just like that she<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/Iloveit_zpsc3e2b260.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401055ra/777805.gif" alt=" photo Iloveit_zpsc3e2b260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>...an instant spark.<br><br><i>
  <b> 'I’ve been looking for you, his eyes are saying. You’ve found me now, I’m certain my eyes are responding.'</b>
</i><br><br> Ha, the fact that her boyfriend is in attendance at this dinner is of no consequence. Conversation flow freely between her and Ian.<br><br><i>
  <b> “Are you really hitting on me with my boyfriend sitting right here?”</b>
</i><b> I am both proud and appalled by his audacity. Scratch that, I am loving his audacity.'</b><br><br><i>
  <b> 'He grabs my hand and kisses it. In that gesture, I feel my childhood slip off of me like an old, worn-out cloak that has been barely hanging by a single thread. I know that something has shifted in me. It’s primal. I want this man.'</b>
</i><br><br>Unfortunately for Michael this is the beginning of the end of his and Sparrow's relationship.<br><br><i>
  <b> “I’m losing you. That’s what’s happening here, right?”</b>
</i> ~Michael<br><br>Ian and Sparrow don't exchange numbers that night at dinner. In fact they come in and out of each others lives for some time. When Ian learns her age he puts the brakes on any budding relationship, Sparrow on the other hand assures him that age is nothing but a number. They've already proven how well they are together even with a 9 close to 10 year age gap. But the age difference is not the only thing working against them; with his busy career which includes tons of traveling and her in school the timing is just not right. So their friendship remains just that "a friendship" for quite a while.<br><br><b> They fall more in to a pattern not a relationship...</b><br>Coming together and linking up.. On top of not hearing from him every few months makes Sparrow question the reality of their on today off tomorrow relationship.<br><br><i>
  <b> '...uneasiness has settled in my gut. Because for all the ways Ian shows me he loves me, he really doesn’t talk about commitment, and he doesn’t demand it of me.'<br><br>'In some ways, it’s possible that I’ve given him the perfect set-up. We have these blissful times every couple of months, and then we both go live our lives apart. How long will this be enough for me?'<br><br>'I try not to be jealous or doubt him, but when we’ve gone four months at a time without seeing each other, during Ian’s overseas tours, it does tend to up the jealousy ante.'</b>
</i><br><br><br>Because of their strong feelings for one another they both decide to make a go for a real relationship. Everything is going good. <b> REAL G O O D</b> . And then just like that your reading and everything... is blown to pieces.<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/used%20gifs%20and%20pics%20for%20book%20reviews/tumblr_inline_miin023rwM1qz4rgp_zps9ac32fde.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401940ra/780724.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_miin023rwM1qz4rgp_zps9ac32fde.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You read and you read until you reach that part where you slowly watch a horrific head on collision happen. You know, you know it will be deadly, leaving no survivors. Well this scene that I read had to be one of THE most effectual scenes...EVER. Not to many female characters are written with an intuition as intense as Sparrow's what's even more intense is that she's had it her whole life. We read how she get's these dreams and feelings that she just doesn't quite understand. And then it happens, she naturally draws a conclusion from her gut.<br><br><b> 'An island of single words strewn together that are going to ruin my entire life. I already know, without him saying a thing, that this will change everything.'</b><br><i>
  <b> “What do you want to know?”</b>
</i> he whispers.<br><i>
  <b> “I want to know everything. Start from the beginning.”</b>
</i><br><br>And even though I knew it was coming, I still thought<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/tears%20tears%20and%20more%20tears/CRYING3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401940ra/780725.gif" alt=" photo CRYING3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>MINOR SPOILERS AHEAD</u><br><br>I felt...every..ounce..of her pain and then some. And then alllll I could hear in my head was the song Resentment by Beyonce. Over and over and over...<br><br><b>I've been crying for too long<br>What did you do to me?<br>I used to be so strong<br>But now you took my soul<br>I'm crying, can't stop crying<br>Can't stop crying....<br>....I know you didn't want to hurt me<br>Look what you've done to me now<br>I gotta look at her in her eyes<br>And see she's had half of me<br>How could you lie?</b><br>- Lyrics Beyonce<br><br>Sparrow's spirit was broken right along with her heart.<br><br>They say time heals wounds.. Well, I'm not sure that's true. What I do know is that L O V E, Love heals wounds.<br><br><i>
  <b>'It came down to love.<br>Love is enough.<br>Love does conquer all.<br>Love really does always protect, trust, hope, persevere…<br>I’d even go as far as saying that love never fails. I finally believe that.'</b>
</i><br> <br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/ee67f7e3-d02d-49d0-bafe-12f0d0ae57f1_zps94385713.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401940i/780726.jpg" alt=" photo ee67f7e3-d02d-49d0-bafe-12f0d0ae57f1_zps94385713.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/a381c05b-2df1-4aa4-9bb6-e725d18620ce_zps5df136c5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401941i/780727.jpg" alt=" photo a381c05b-2df1-4aa4-9bb6-e725d18620ce_zps5df136c5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b><u>CASTING:</u> Meet my Sparrow and Ian</b><br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/6a25fbf6-fae2-4c7d-a276-3fd15f1bdec0_zpsd0b3b3b4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401941i/780728.jpg" alt=" photo 6a25fbf6-fae2-4c7d-a276-3fd15f1bdec0_zpsd0b3b3b4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/dbcb0d4a-4f45-45a1-84f0-e3e666e163c2_zps5e5870e3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401941i/780729.jpg" alt=" photo dbcb0d4a-4f45-45a1-84f0-e3e666e163c2_zps5e5870e3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>Willow Aster has a way with words I was completely sucked in by her style it appealed to me in a way that not most authors are able to do. Her characters just popped off the pages I couldn't seem to get enough! I fell so hard for these characters. The only thing that stopped me from giving this book 5 stars is the fact that I felt like I missed out on vital information. Mainly due to the fact we get everything from Sparrow's pov. I wanted to know more about Laila and her reasons for being a cold hearted slimy BITCH. I wanted more details on how things went down between Ian and Laila the night he finally explains it readers don't get the grimly details. We don't get to know his thought process... I don't know maybe that's just me wanting all the deets.<br><br>I really enjoyed the secondary characters, which leads me to ask..<br>What I really want to know is... Will Jeff and Laila get a book?<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Lovable<br>Writing Style- Excellent<br>Plot/Storyline- Intense and Highly emotional<br>Steam Factor- Medium/Moderately Steamy<br>Overall- I loved it! READ IT!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539900185?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539900185" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12319676855961567480"><a href='http://beta.photobucket.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410238i/804141.jpg' alt=' photo truelovestoryquote1_zps44c73ab3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>This is how it begins. </b><br/><br/>Ian Sterling has broken Sparrow’s heart into a million tiny little pieces and destroyed her faith in love. She’s spotted him in an airport and is trying to avoid him but he knows she is there and is not about to let this opportunity pass him by. He’s desperate to get her back – he’s desperate for her forgiveness.<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“I see this face every night when I close my eyes. All day long, I think I see you, everywhere I go…” His eyes cloud, and he drops his hands. “I’ve dreamed </blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText12319676855961567480" style="display:none"><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410238i/804141.jpg" alt=" photo truelovestoryquote1_zps44c73ab3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>This is how it begins. </b><br><br>Ian Sterling has broken Sparrow’s heart into a million tiny little pieces and destroyed her faith in love. She’s spotted him in an airport and is trying to avoid him but he knows she is there and is not about to let this opportunity pass him by. He’s desperate to get her back – he’s desperate for her forgiveness.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I see this face every night when I close my eyes. All day long, I think I see you, everywhere I go…” His eyes cloud, and he drops his hands. “I’ve dreamed this so many times, I’m not even sure you’re real right now. Are you really here?”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>We jump straight back to the past, five years, eleven months, and one day ago to the moment they first meet. Sparrow is young, very young, daughter of a preacher, on the verge of heading off to college in New York and everyone is hoping she will settle down with Michael – her nice, safe boyfriend. And in walks Ian Sterling. And everything changes. Nothing will <b>EVER</b> be the same again for Sparrow.<br><br>Their connection is instant and undeniable and they can hardly keep their eyes off one another and they meet again a few days later and they both realise that this is special but Ian is almost ten years older than Sparrow and, as a travelling musician, he’s not what Sparrow’s parents have in mind and so Ian attempts to do the noble thing and stay away from her.<br><br>Over the years they bump into one another several times, that all-consuming, sizzling attraction is not to be denied and they grow closer and closer but Ian is evasive and they don’t really forge a connection until several years have gone by. By this time, it’s apparent that they are completely in love with one another and, eventually, everyone around them accepts them as a couple but not everything is as it seems and I got to the point when I decided that Ian most definitely needed a good bitchslap.<br><br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410238ra/804142.gif" alt=" photo battery.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I sure hope that hurt!! You deserved it!!<br><br>I loved Sparrow – she may be innocent at the beginning of the story but she’s ready to leave her conservative past behind her and start life anew in New York. She’s full of hope, expectation and has an unmistakable joie de vivre. I loved her humour and her quirkiness. Ian – I did love him despite the urge to cause him physical pain. He’s funny, caring, sexy and ultimately fucked up. He’s got a lot to learn from Sparrow and the lessons are going to be slow and hard and painful.<br><br>This was just such a beautiful and highly realistic love story. It takes place over several years and tells the simple tale of boy meets girl, boy and girl fall in love and boy fucks up monumentally. It’s such a soulful story – as a reader, I felt every deep emotion with Sparrow. There was excitement, lust, anxiety, supreme happiness and the depths of despair. It’s just one of those stories that grabs you by the heart and doesn’t let go and you’re dragged along, completely unable to look away, however hard it is to keep watching. It’s emotional, compelling and I absolutely devoured it.<br><br>Highly accomplished and highly recommended debut novel from Willow Aster. I’ll definitely be looking for more from this author in the future.<br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410238i/804143.jpg" alt=" photo truelvequote1_zps1a4d8941.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>4.5 beautiful stars</b><br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

<div id="review_541309065" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/541309065" />
    <a title="Belle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9419782-belle"><img alt="Belle" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/541309065?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Belle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Belle" href="/user/show/9419782-belle">Belle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer541309065" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4265373839965991450"><b> GEH IAN WHY.. JUST WHY..<br/><br/>F*** sorry I am about to start an ENORMOUS RANT. So bare with me </b><br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/>I get the whole . . . age difference/ he didn't feel he deserved her.. but an ONGOING affair throughout basically their ENTIRE relationship. I wish we got more details about the affair, like if it happened often or saw his point of view, I mean just how far did the affair go?.. i wish i could have been there for the hushed fighting conversations between Laila and Ian. How could he cheat right</span></span>
  <span id="freeText4265373839965991450" style="display:none"><b> GEH IAN WHY.. JUST WHY..<br /><br />F*** sorry I am about to start an ENORMOUS RANT. So bare with me </b><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />I get the whole . . . age difference/ he didn't feel he deserved her.. but an ONGOING affair throughout basically their ENTIRE relationship. I wish we got more details about the affair, like if it happened often or saw his point of view, I mean just how far did the affair go?.. i wish i could have been there for the hushed fighting conversations between Laila and Ian. How could he cheat right AFTER he proposed and they were finally exclusive. Sure they didnt have sex, but HE STILL CHEATED. That whole part of the storyline I saw coming a mile away, as soon as I saw how Laila treated Ian, but man I really wished it didn't. It just ruined Ian in my eyes to be honest. Yes, I believed he loved her. But what, was he just never going to tell her the truth ? Sure in the beginning, they were not exclusive, but Ian not only ruined his relationship, but how could he ruin his own cousins ? His own flesh and blood ? That betrayal, I have no clue how Jeff could move past that. If my best friend, and cousin slept with my wife... man, unforgivable. What is worse, is that Ian and Laila did not even love each other.. just used each other for sex. So really the whole affair was completely unjustified. Ian should have talked to Sparrow not jumped into bed with his cousin's wife. <br /><br />Before the revelation I saw coming but really did not want to happen, I would have WHOLEHEARTEDLY given this book a 4.5.. dare I say a 5/5 but after that .. it dropped to a 1.5. I will say SURE cheating is reality. And yes, I have tolerated cheating in books when it comes to being committed and in love with the other person and the very rare circumstances that makes it somewhat easier to digest. But when two characters cheat for the sake of cheating, I will never ever be okay with reading it. I was really proud of how Sparrow handled it, and I'm glad she got her happy ending. In saying that, Ian really did not deserve to get his. Am I being a cold hearted bitch ? Probably, but the whole way it was handled and how he was never planning on telling her made me sick to the core. Yeah he definitely felt remorse, and he paid for it, but there is just something in me that still won't accept the fact that he cheated throughout their entire relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />In saying all that I will say this book will definitely fall into many people's category of a great romance novel. So this is entirely MY SOLE opinion. So don't listen to me.. read for yourself and make up your own mind. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4265373839965991450" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_520177888" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/520177888" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/520177888?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites-of-all-time">favorites-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=ebooks-i-own-not-bn">ebooks-i-own-not-bn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=cheating">cheating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=make-me-cry">make-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=self-contained">self-contained</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=new-authors-review">new-authors-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-new-adult">genre-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer520177888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15434974472919830166"><b>Want to read a True <s>Love</s> Story? Here it is!!! It's heartbreaking and intense, gut churning and real. It hurt to read, it laid me out but kept me up all night. I read this book in one sitting.</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407014i/794643._SX540_.jpg' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was captivated by this like nothing I've been captivated by in quite some time. Something, some elusive quality, grabbed me...the title, the cover...something made me burn for this book as soon as I noticed it. And it paid off. I freaking LOVED this book!<br/><br/>First off, the blurb is really misleadi</span>
  <span id="freeText15434974472919830166" style="display:none"><b>Want to read a True <s>Love</s> Story? Here it is!!! It's heartbreaking and intense, gut churning and real. It hurt to read, it laid me out but kept me up all night. I read this book in one sitting.</b><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407014i/794643._SX540_.jpg" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was captivated by this like nothing I've been captivated by in quite some time. Something, some elusive quality, grabbed me...the title, the cover...something made me burn for this book as soon as I noticed it. And it paid off. I freaking LOVED this book!<br><br>First off, the blurb is really misleading, at least for me. I thought that it was some weird mess-with-your-mind game of chance and oddity. But it's just a plain ole contemporary romance about circumstances and mutual acquaintance throwing this couple together every few months, and their inexplicable attraction to each other.<br><br>Maybe attraction is too tame a word. Sparrow and Ian are <i>connected</i>. From their first face to face meeting, the chemistry and invisible line between them is so palpable, if set my tummy butterflies off immediately. <br><br>But this is NOT an insta-love story. This is an insta-connect story. This is a story about two people who are meant to be together, but life gets in the way. Age, location, vocation, time, family, friends, and most of all their own reluctance and eventual <b>stupidity</b> are blocking their path to each other.<br><br>When the story starts, it's already heartbreaking:<br><br><b>"It has been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him. Two years, ten months, and five days since he broke my heart - well, since I <i>knew</i> he had broken my heart. Technically, he began breaking my heart the moment I met him."</b><br><br>Sparrow is a precher's daughter. The proverbial good girl next door, she has a strong sense of faith and purpose. But she's not holier than thou, she's just a normal girl getting ready to move away from home to go to college, looking forward to wearing what she wants and discovering what it is to be responsible for your own life. One day, her family goes to dinner with some friends...just another day, but it's the day that changes her life.<br><br>She meets Ian Sterling.<br><br>Ian is an up and coming guitarist and singer. Sparrow had actually seen him play years ago, before his name was known, and had a little girl's crush on him ever since. But now, the crush isn't so little any more. Ian is flirty and charming, but more than that, they both know without a doubt that there's something extra there between them. If only....all of those obstacles were gone. But they're not. <br><br>Over then next couple of years, Ian and Sparrow spend minute amounts of time together whenever fate sees fit to allow it. And each time, a deeper bond is forged, and their inevitable love blooms. It's powerful, and it's beautiful. Ian and Sparrow as a couple are perfection. They laugh together...boy, these two can be goofy! Their chemistry is off the charts, but it's not an overtly sexual relationship for a very long time. They just fit, like puzzle pieces. <br><br><b>"You have this grounding quality about you. I don't know a better way to put it. It levels me. I've never been at home anywhere, but I am with you."</b><br><br>And in step those obstacles...mainly stupidity. How do you say I'm sorry for betrayal? When you know nothing you say will erase what you've done....<br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407217i/795138._SX540_.jpg" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>God, it made me hurt!!! This true <s>love</s> story brought me down and yanked the tears right out of me. I gasped out loud, even though I KNEW it was coming...I KNEW IT for the entire book!!!! How did I fall so in love, how did Sparrow fall so in love? You can't help it. If ever lovers have been star crossed, it's these two. They're just so perfect together and hopeless apart. <br><br><b>"I sent him away.<br>I'm mad that he went.<br>I can't love him.<br>I can't hate him either.<br>Ian Sterling has ruined me. And he's ruined me for anyone else."</b><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407217i/795139.jpg" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And how do you move on from losing the love of your life...knowing, <b>KNOWING</b> that you've both lost it all?<br><br>I love this author's voice. She writes with such heart, and the inner dialogue of Sparrow is hilarious. The girl thinks in jokes at times, and constantly kept me on my toes. Watching Sparrow grow into a woman, from age eighteen to twenty four....those formative years in which so much happens...she grows so much as a person. And how often do you truly find your soulmate so early in life? And really KNOW it?! She knows it. And that makes the betrayal all the more heartbreaking. The fact that I can forgive is quite phenomenal, but I did. <br><br>What a gorgeous story...and it's completely self contained, with a short but fabulous epilogue. Beautiful, wonderful story penned by Willow Aster. I am sold on anything you may ever write again!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15434974472919830166" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_485373173" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/485373173" />
    <a title="Jenny Levine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12673270-jenny-levine"><img alt="Jenny Levine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353067785p2/12673270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/485373173?book_show_action=true">Dec 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny Levine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny Levine" href="/user/show/12673270-jenny-levine">Jenny Levine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12673270-jenny-levine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485373173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12786412539433135535"><blockquote> <b> I’ve been looking for you, his eyes are saying.<br/>You’ve found me now, I’m certain my eyes are responding. </b> </blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401838ra/780430.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Sparrow Kate--</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/>Always been the perfect daughter, now she has transformed --starting with the way she dresses and expressing herself. And her life gets much more interesting when she met the man who will turn her life upside down...<br/><br/><b> Ian Sterling--</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>A professional musician. Player. Womanizer.<br/>But, all because he fears rejection and fears being in a relationship.<br/>If there</span>
  <span id="freeText12786412539433135535" style="display:none"><blockquote> <b> I’ve been looking for you, his eyes are saying.<br>You’ve found me now, I’m certain my eyes are responding. </b> </blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401838ra/780430.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Sparrow Kate--</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br>Always been the perfect daughter, now she has transformed --starting with the way she dresses and expressing herself. And her life gets much more interesting when she met the man who will turn her life upside down...<br><br><b> Ian Sterling--</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>A professional musician. Player. Womanizer.<br>But, all because he fears rejection and fears being in a relationship.<br>If there's one word to describe him, it would be -- T.R.O.U.B.L.E!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402023ra/781086.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But, she wants him since she first laid her eyes on him.<br>And, he wants her too.<br><br>I'll remind you though, he's <b> <u> TROUBLE</u>! </b><br><br>BUT,<br>How can she deny his feelings for him?<br>How can he deny the attraction he has for her?<br><br>Will it work even though he isn't a relationship type of guy?<br><br><b> <i> WILL LOVE BE ENOUGH? </i> </b><br><br>When they actually become a couple and with Ian going on tour, will a long distance relationship work?<br><br><b> <i> IS LOVE GOING TO BE ENOUGH? </i> </b><br><br>But, when he did something terrible and unforgivable to compromise their relationship, what will happen to them?<br>Does he deserve her forgiveness?<br><br><b> <i> IS LOVE STILL ENOUGH? </i></b> <br>Sparrow,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402023ra/781087.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A beautiful story about letting go but still holding on to the love they both had for one another...<br>Steadfast love...<br>A story about second chances... of never losing hope.<br>A story about<br><i> Holding on.<br>Breaking down.<br>Opening up.<br>Hurting.<br>Healing... </i><br>This is <u> Sparrow and Ian</u>'s <b> TRUE <s>LOVE</s> STORY. </b><br><br><u> Warning: Spoilers ahead. Read at your own risk. </u><br><br>Hi! I'm back!<br>This review will start off with my complaints.<br><br>Two words: <b> Cover Fail </b><br>Am I the only one who has a problem with the cover? I think it's misleading. I don't really get it or it's connection with the story. I thought this is a paranormal romance book. LOL.<br>And then, when I read the first line of the blurb and it says: <i> Sparrow Kate is transforming, </i> I said to myself, <i> Yep, this is PNR. </i> I thought this book's about zombies or vampires, but when I read some of my friends' reviews, this was actually a romance novel. Stupid me for not reading the entire blurb. Lesson learned.<br><br>Moving on...<br><br><blockquote> <b> SHOOT! HOLY CRACK! THIS BOOK IS EFFIN' GOOD!!! </b> </blockquote><br>I love the author's writing style, like she has a way of getting the readers hooked at the first <s>chapter</s> line of the book...I know I did. The story actually began in present time, a year, two months, and seventeen days since she last saw him. Two years, ten months, and five days since he broke her heart--when they bump into each other in the airport. And then, the next chapter jumps back in the past and tells us how it all started and what went wrong. I love it! Plus, the titles in each chapter are just brilliant.<br><br>Sparrow - what a lovely and unique name. (The author got her surname from author Tarryn Fisher, right? Cool.) Another heroine who should be congratulated for having a famous vagina. Yeah, she's popular with the guys. They all seem smitten with her. But, I love her because she's smart and funny. And when she's with Ian, ahhh, perfect :)<br><br>Ian Orville Sterling, yes, I know he's an asshole, and when he did that horrible thing to Sparrow and fvck up their relationship, I was like, Ian,<br><span>[image error]</span><br>and when they <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ broke up and their love life were in shambles  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, my heart broke for them.<br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>But you know what? I still love him. Why? All his lines are like asdfkglskfdhsl, took my breath away. *sigh* How can you not fall in love? Most of my fave quotes from the book are said by Ian. And my favorite part? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The endless letters. For me, they're the highlight of the book.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> OMFG. My heart hurts a lot just reading it.<br><br>Sparrow and Ian -- DANGGGG! These two are made for each other. Off the charts chemistry. I love it when Ian calls Sparrow "Little Bird." And their lines and banters are perfection. *sigh*<br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><b> “You’re impossible.”<br>“You’re delectable.”<br>“You’re incorrigible.”<br>“You’re edible.”<br><br>I say, “What do you like about me besides my looks?”<br>“The fact that you would ask me something like that is a clear indication of the kind of person you are, Sparrow Fisher. You have this grounding quality about you. I don’t know a better way to put it. It levels me. I’ve never been at home anywhere, but I am with you.”<br><br>“You’re an angel.”<br>“You’re trouble,” I laugh.<br>“I can’t keep my hands off you,” he says.<br>“I don’t want you to.”<br><br>“I want to be who you think I am.”<br>“I want you to be who you are.” </b><br><br>I wish the epilogue could've been longer though. Or idk, I think it's just an excuse because I want more.<br><br>Also, I don't like the name <i> Ianow Orvillate </i>.<br><br>My favorite Ian letter:<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ We Belong Together.<br>Well, Baby—Think.<br>Words Beginning Thus Would Be<br>Tender Words—But True.<br>Wonderful, Beautiful, Thoughtful Words,<br>But They Would Be Truthful Words.Believe Them.<br>Wishes Become True.<br>Wisdom Brings Trust.<br>We’re Being Tested.<br>We’re Both Tough.<br>Who Buys That?<br>Waiting By Telephone.<br>Wake Before Twelve.<br>Work Before Television.<br>Wiggle Big Toe.<br>Well … Be Thinking<br>Warm-Blooded Teddy<br>World’s Biggest Turkey<br>Way Back Then<br>Warm Bellies Touched<br>We Began Trembling<br>Weeping Boy Thinks,<br>“Where’s Baby’s Touch?”<br>What Big Tears.<br>We Belong Together.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b> Overall </b>, IAN AND SPARROW DO BELONG TOGETHER. And I'm happy of their HEA and I love reading their story so much. This will go straight to my favorites ;)<br><br>At the end of the road for Sparrow and Ian though---<br><br><blockquote> <b> "Love is enough.<br>Love does conquer all.<br>Love really does always protect, trust, hope, persevere...<br>I'd even go as far as saying that love never fails.<br>I finally believe that." </b> </blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402023ra/781091.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My advice for y'all? <b> STOP WHAT YOU'RE DOING AND READ THIS BOOK! </b><br><br><b> 4.5 SECOND CHANCE STARS! </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
