<div id="review_539819193" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/539819193" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539819193?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539819193" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12868744609793454379"><b>5 Beautiful Heart-Shattering Stars!!! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/9a0d1a91-7c7d-41eb-884f-7e02bf6eab77_zps1d6635ed.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/803997.jpg' alt=' photo 9a0d1a91-7c7d-41eb-884f-7e02bf6eab77_zps1d6635ed.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I loved Sparrow and Ian’s story. Loved it. I spent a good 20-25% of the book crying, but what a fantastic read!<br/><br/><b>
  <i> It’s been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him. Two years, ten months and five days since he broke my heart.</i>
</b>  The story starts out five years after Sparrow and Ian’s initial meeting. A few years ago, the love of her life completely shattered Sparrow’s heart. Ian is still not over Sparrow, in fact, he may never be. The</span>
  <span id="freeText12868744609793454379" style="display:none"><b>5 Beautiful Heart-Shattering Stars!!! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/9a0d1a91-7c7d-41eb-884f-7e02bf6eab77_zps1d6635ed.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/803997.jpg" alt=" photo 9a0d1a91-7c7d-41eb-884f-7e02bf6eab77_zps1d6635ed.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved Sparrow and Ian’s story. Loved it. I spent a good 20-25% of the book crying, but what a fantastic read!<br><br><b>
  <i> It’s been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him. Two years, ten months and five days since he broke my heart.</i>
</b>  The story starts out five years after Sparrow and Ian’s initial meeting. A few years ago, the love of her life completely shattered Sparrow’s heart. Ian is still not over Sparrow, in fact, he may never be. They happen to run into each other at the airport and as luck would have it, they are seated together on the same flight. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/TrueLoveStory-breakyourheartedit_zpsb784548c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/803998.jpg" alt=" photo TrueLoveStory-breakyourheartedit_zpsb784548c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>We get to go back in time when Sparrow and Ian first met. She is about 18, he is a bit older than that... Sparrow is a pastor’s daughter who is getting ready to go to NYC to school. She wants to be an author. Ian is a musician. They have a connection, a spark from the very beginning. Because of the age difference, and Ian’s reputation as a ladies man, he is hesitant to be with her. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/d6b5f5a5-7adc-4a53-8e9e-5424cc1f562f_zpsfa5b49cf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/803999._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo d6b5f5a5-7adc-4a53-8e9e-5424cc1f562f_zpsfa5b49cf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/1b9fb9cf-1c32-4a48-98c0-1f31e55a5dd3_zpsfc747618.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/804000._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1b9fb9cf-1c32-4a48-98c0-1f31e55a5dd3_zpsfc747618.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They can’t deny the connection they have, the spark. These two have some major chemistry and very strong feelings for each other. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/TrueLoveStory-kissingedit_zps98f70cb0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/804001.jpg" alt=" photo TrueLoveStory-kissingedit_zps98f70cb0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Eventually, after a year or so of friendship and seeing each other when convenient, they decide to attempt a real relationship. It is difficult with the long distance, Ian is always on tour. But she’s in love with him, he loves her too. They try to make it work, despite all the obstacles. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/TrueLoveStory-Playfuledit_zpsdc27a0ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/804002.jpg" alt=" photo TrueLoveStory-Playfuledit_zpsdc27a0ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ian has issues with himself. He never feels like he is good enough to be with Sparrow, but she loves him for who he is and always tries to make him feel worthy of her love. Things are going pretty great for the two of them. They are getting ready to make a pretty big commitment to each other and Sparrow couldn’t be happier. That is until around the 77% mark...... <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Faultinourstars-sadface_zpsc13cfb1c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/516011.gif" alt=" photo Faultinourstars-sadface_zpsc13cfb1c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Devastation. No other word for it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I was SOOO upset with this turn in the book! I mean, seriously?!?!?! I loved Ian. I mean LOVED him! I really couldn’t believe he could do this to Sparrow. Maybe if it would have been when they were first together before they had the exclusivity talk, I wouldn’t have been so upset, but really? And with that bitch? I just don’t get it... I don’t get it.... End Rant lol <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Sparrow was devastated. Ian was devastated. I was devastated. It was just all around terrible. Then came all of the letters. A tear fest. No matter what Ian does or says, Sparrow doesn’t think she will ever be able to get over his betrayal. They are both miserable. This goes on for years. Can you ever get over your one true love???<br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/TrueLovestory-walkingawayedit_zpsad87f943.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/804003.jpg" alt=" photo TrueLovestory-walkingawayedit_zpsad87f943.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sparrow and Ian were two pretty awesome main characters. Sparrow is young. She is fun, sweet and innocent. She gets to be independent for the first time in her life. Loved watching her journey. She made some mistakes, but learned from them. Oh Ian. Ian, Ian, Ian... don’t know what to do with him. I know a lot of readers might not care for Ian- but despite all of his screw ups, I still love him! He is flawed, self depreciating, but also caring, loving, funny and sexy. The main reason I loved Ian <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Even though he did something so terrible and awful, I really felt he learned from it. He did what he did, but he tried to make up for it. He stayed faithful to Sparrow all that time- even when they weren’t together. He redeemed himself in my eyes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I also loved the nick name... Little bird- how sweet!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/7dc4ece8-a882-4203-ba7e-9d90d64bb2de_zps3238d935.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/804004.jpg" alt=" photo 7dc4ece8-a882-4203-ba7e-9d90d64bb2de_zps3238d935.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story was captivating from the very beginning. A beautiful and emotional story. I smiled a lot, laughed, cried and sobbed. I loved it. And for anyone hesitant to read it, don’t worry... The ending is perfect. There is no cliffhanger, and the last few pages will leave you with a smile on your face. This one is for sure going right on the favorites shelf! Ian and Sparrow are one of those couples that just belong together. <b>READ IT!!!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/TrueLoveStory-Neverends_zpsea1cc790.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410225i/804005._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo TrueLoveStory-Neverends_zpsea1cc790.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12868744609793454379" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer16560176097414771814"><b>Short review finally posted. <br/><br/>3 to 3 1/2 Stars.</b><br/><br/>The only cheating plot-line that's HEA I believed. Still, I hate cheating plot-lines and didn't realize I was reading one until it was too late (I should have paid more attention to the reviews). Overall, <i>True Love Story</i> is a well written, captivating, and very angsty book. <br/><br/>Note: The fact I gave a cheating plot-line a 3 to 3 1/2 star rating says something! I hate them. </span>

<div id="review_484663134" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484663134" />
    <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz"><img alt="Elizabeth (Liz)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551206872p2/5495317.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/484663134?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Liz)" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz">Elizabeth (Liz)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=5-star-reads">5-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=ebook-read">ebook-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=contemporary-romance-read">contemporary-romance-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=arc-from-author-read">arc-from-author-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=to-be-reviewed">to-be-reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer484663134" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17376202253169190367">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><br/>Genre: New Adult/Contemporary<br/><br/>Heat Level: Medium<br/><br/>Angst Level: Angsty, but nothing OTT<br/><br/>Warnings: Cheating (it's an admission of cheating, but we don't 'watch' it happen)<br/><br/><br/><br/>5 Stars<br/><br/>True Love Story is an amazingly honest and emotionally complete journey! It is a journey that is so worth taking with Sparrow and Ian. <br/><br/>This is a simple story. Sparrow Fisher is a pastor's daughter, growing up outside of San Francisco. When we first meet her, she is eighteen years old, inc</span>
  <span id="freeText17376202253169190367" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><br />Genre: New Adult/Contemporary<br /><br />Heat Level: Medium<br /><br />Angst Level: Angsty, but nothing OTT<br /><br />Warnings: Cheating (it's an admission of cheating, but we don't 'watch' it happen)<br /><br /><br /><br />5 Stars<br /><br />True Love Story is an amazingly honest and emotionally complete journey! It is a journey that is so worth taking with Sparrow and Ian. <br /><br />This is a simple story. Sparrow Fisher is a pastor's daughter, growing up outside of San Francisco. When we first meet her, she is eighteen years old, incredibly sheltered and naive, in some ways terribly old-fashioned, and soon to be starting NYU. Ian Sterling is boyish (though nine years older than Sparrow), charming, handsome and riddled with hangups and insecurities. He is a musical hero of Sparrow's, and, as a cousin to a friend of her father, the two first meet prior to her leaving for college. The chemistry and attraction between the two is near-instant and very easy. However, the possibility of a relationship seems anything but. What follows over the next five years are the ups and downs of attempting to build that relationship, make it work, and find out if love really can conquer all. <br /><br /><br />As I said, True Love Story is a simple story...deceptively so. Why? Because any time human emotions are involved, simple becomes complex. True Love Story is a perfect example of this. Girl and boy meet, spend a beautiful day together, and realize immediately that something magical is happening between them. What comes next should be obvious and uncomplicated, shouldn't it? Oh, but life rarely works that way. Now, this storyline certainly isn't a new one, BUT, Willow Aster expertly took it, made it her own, and brought it to new life. This book truly has everything we should demand in a great, 5-star read. The author gives us depth, emotion, chemistry, character growth, good dialog, subtle humor, and a maturity of writing ability and style that we don't often find in a debut.<br /><br />The two most important elements in True Love Story are the characters of Sparrow Fisher and Ian Sterling. The focus is exclusively on them throughout this book. Through these two characters the author makes us feel and live the depth of emotion and chemistry between the two. We find the humor in their banter and re-explore life lessons through their serious conversations. Best of all, we watch the evolution of two immature individuals--one youthful, sheltered and naive, the other older, insecure and afraid of commitment. The character growth in this story is amazing, and most obviously evident in Sparrow. In the beginning, it is almost painful how innocent and a bit odd she is. But, it is beautiful to watch her blossom from awkward young adult to fully-grown, experienced woman...even if the path is difficult. Maybe, *especially* because the path is difficult. Ian's road is no less bumpy, and to witness the man he becomes is a lovely thing.<br /><br />True Love Story is a *real* love story, just as the title indicates, with warts and all. We almost have to close the book to fully realize the journey we just walked with these two characters. Their love is all-encompassing. By the end, the love is so tangible we can almost reach out and touch it. The epilogue is PERFECTION, and the book would not have been complete without it!<br /><br />In the end, what this is, is a beautifully human story told by a wonderful new voice in the romance genre. Bravo, Willow Aster!! <br /><br /><br /><br /><br />**Copy provided by the author in exchange for an honest review**</span>
  <a data-text-id="17376202253169190367" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_541355312" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/541355312" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/541355312?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=my-friend-anna-and-her-weepy-reads">my-friend-anna-and-her-weepy-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer541355312" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7591709578413816728">5 TRUE LOVE STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410455i/804802._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='460' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Willow Aster, has written a beautifully put together, engaging love story. My usual type of romance is normally sugar coated and laced with predictability. This novel is a little more realistic with its approach to real love, and I was sold.<br/><br/>This is the story of Sparrow and Ian a couple who complete each other, who fall in love over and over again like they can't survive without each other. They don't like, they love. The book takes the reader on a journey of hearts, leading you</span>
  <span id="freeText7591709578413816728" style="display:none">5 TRUE LOVE STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410455i/804802._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Willow Aster, has written a beautifully put together, engaging love story. My usual type of romance is normally sugar coated and laced with predictability. This novel is a little more realistic with its approach to real love, and I was sold.<br><br>This is the story of Sparrow and Ian a couple who complete each other, who fall in love over and over again like they can't survive without each other. They don't like, they love. The book takes the reader on a journey of hearts, leading you to believe that they cant spend the rest of their lives without each other, but life happens, heartache and deception take root and this is their story ... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410455i/804803._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was 'True Lisa Loving' of this book and here's why ... Great build up to a meaningful relationship, fabulous inner monologue from the gorgeous heroine. Compelling story telling - I was swept up from chapter to chapter in the story. The characters all had their perfect place, from the parents, to the friends to this books version of a wicked witch, I was drawn in and excited to pick this book up when I could. <br><br>This story has so many beautifully descriptive parts to make it a wonderful reading experience. This book has a bit of everything, true love, lonely hearts, heart ache and break, reconciliation, faith, friendship and much more.<br><br>I loved everything about Sparrow and Ian's relationship as flawed as it was, I cheered for their much deserved Love forever ending. There's not many times I can truly say I loved a female character in a book, here I did. Sparrow is a character I'll not soon forget. Ian captured my heart, even as self destructive as he was, my heart broke for him. This author has a raw talent of bringing her characters to life and I applaud her.<br><br>❤❤"It has been a year, two months, and seventeen days since I last saw him. Two years, ten months, and five days since he broke my heart."<br><br>❤❤"I've never been at home anywhere but I am with you."<br><br>❤❤"I drink him in and I know my fate is sealed: I am his."<br><br>❤❤"I'm yours, Sparrow. if you'll have me, I'm yours."<br><br>❤❤"I want to be who you think I am."<br>"I want you to be who you are."<br><br>❤❤"my soul is knit to yours. My life is hinged to yours. I move, I breathe, but I don't really live without you. All that keeps my heart beating is the hope that it will someday beat next to yours again."<br><br>I truly love and recommend this story to all. I have a serious case of the warm and fuzzies towards this obviously talented author, and I'll be eagerly looking out (stalking) for future books.<br><br>Read on, friends ... You won't regret.<br><br>5 well earned stars.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410455i/804804._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7591709578413816728" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_484518779" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484518779" />
    <a title=".Lili. " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8905618-lili"><img alt=".Lili. " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593508329p2/8905618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

  <b>Can't We All Agree to Just Agree</b>

Little Bird you are the most beautiful girl I've ever seen in my life!! I'm going to start calling you Little Bird because that's what a sparrow is, right? And with Sparrow being your name and all, it sounds perfect!! Not that the name Sparrow sounds a tad contrived or silly. And you know, I do write songs which sell millions of copies so it probably sounds very poetic and maybe a little emo.<br /><br /><b>Sparrow:</b> Oh no, Ian! You are the most handsome, most talented, bestest boyfriend, EVAH!!! It doesn't even matter that you blow into town, sweet talk me and get me all hot and bothered for a few hours then leave and never call or email or text for 2 or 3 months. I carry the memory of your perfection in my heart, always!<br /><br /><b>Ian:</b> Sparrow, your smile just lights up the whole fucking world!! I know I'm not the only one who thinks that. Shit, I know everyone, and I mean <b>EVERYONE</b>, who meets you falls in love with you within 30 seconds of seeing you. Come to think of it, only men who see you fall for you. You don't seem to meet a lot of women but at least your besty from California likes you. Well, and your mom, though she kinda has to. Though, for some reason, my cousin's wife, Laila, doesn't. Hmmmm...I wonder why...<br /><br /><b>Sparrow:</b> Ian! Ian! (snaps her fingers in his face) Back to me! You know I can't say curse words because I'm a preacher's daughter, but if I could, I would tell you that your hair just fuckin' rocks!!! Oh! Did I just say a curse word? Gosh, I hope God doesn't strike me down! Naaaw...he won't because I am one of his perfect creations and so beautiful that it would just be a crying shame if that happened.<br /><br /><b>Ian:</b> Sparrow, your fashion sense is the bomb! You are the cat's meow, the bee's knees, the <b>ULTIMATE</b> fashionista now that you've moved to NYC and get to shop with your daddy's congregation's donations and wear those ultra skin-tight, brightly colored, cut-up-to-your-perfect-ass dresses and ski bunny suits!!! Boy if those people could see you now, they would be in fucking awe of your beauty! And I'm pretty sure they think it was money well spent to send you out of state to go to a university in NEW YORK CITY!! Because...well...you're perfect which anyone can see.<br /><br /><b>Sparrow:</b> Oh, Ian. You are the most perfect, most beautiful, most well-modulated voiced boyfriend I've ever had!!! Did I tell you your hair is perfect? I did? Well, just let me tell you again! And again! And again! You're hair is sooooo perfect!!<br /><br /><b>Ian:</b> Please marry me, Little Bird, and make me the happiest, cheating, stalking, dirt-sucking, scumbag, douche bag, dickwad, piece of shit in the whole entire universe!! <br /><br /><b>Sparrow (squeeing):</b> Oh Ian!! Yes! Yes! Yes! I will marry you!!! Omigod!! Wait! <div id="review_517497258" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/517497258" />
    <a title="Joan (official heroine hater)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater"><img alt="Joan (official heroine hater)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397098767p2/4910112.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/517497258?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Joan (official heroine hater)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Joan (official heroine hater)" href="/user/show/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater">Joan (official heroine hater)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">no one</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater?shelf=just-god-awful">just-god-awful</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater?shelf=heroine-hatred">heroine-hatred</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater?shelf=on-kindle">on-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4910112-joan-official-heroine-hater?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer517497258" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1464521189024542849">I’m not sure where to even begin with this book. There seems to a general outpouring of love for it but I’m afraid I just wasn’t feeling it...AT ALL! <br/>I’ll admit to being a total heroine hater most of the time. The smallest thing can set me off with these chicks and they quickly find themselves on my sh*t list. Usually, though, I’m still able to swoon over the heroes or at least feel sorry for them that they have to put up with these clueless bimbos. I’m afraid that wasn’t the case here, no, I wa</span>
  <span id="freeText1464521189024542849" style="display:none">I’m not sure where to even begin with this book. There seems to a general outpouring of love for it but I’m afraid I just wasn’t feeling it...AT ALL! <br />I’ll admit to being a total heroine hater most of the time. The smallest thing can set me off with these chicks and they quickly find themselves on my sh*t list. Usually, though, I’m still able to swoon over the heroes or at least feel sorry for them that they have to put up with these clueless bimbos. I’m afraid that wasn’t the case here, no, I was feeling the hate for both characters in this one. There was just something off about Ian from the very get-go and he kept up his downward spiral as he smirked, grinned, tugged his hair and man whored his way through. And at about the 50% mark, we get the male angst and self-loathing. Man, this guy could give Edward Cullen a run for his money. Of course, he’s supposed to be hot, though we’re never really given much of a physical description except for the odd quote of “cushiony lips” several times. Um, ew? What exactly are “cushiony lips” pray tell? I just kept thinking of the throw pillows on my couch…<br /> Then there is Sparrow, our heroine… We are told repeatedly and over and over and over again that this girl is beautiful, gorgeous, a vision, electrifying and my person favorite “have you ever thought of modeling for Victoria’s Secret?”. Literally, every man that crosses paths with this girl tells her how beautiful she is-I’m NOT kidding. So, I’m wondering…do men really do this? Do they just blurt out to perfect strangers/attractive women how beautiful they are? Because, wow, I guess I’ve been missing out since I’m afraid I don’t look like a runway/swimsuit model myself….sucks to be me! To make this book more interesting, I really should have kept a running tally of just how many times Sparrow is told she’s gorgeous, but alas, I didn’t. If I had to make an estimate though, I’d say at least 50+. Oh, and that’s not all! No, no, she’s also “smart” and “FUNNY’! We are told constantly that people are literally in tears laughing at the things that come out of her mouth. Meanwhile, I’m sitting there reading all these things and not even cracking a smile….guess you had to be there?<br />So, enough about the characters, what about the plot you ask? Basically, by the end of the first chapter you know EXACTLY where this story is going to go and it’s just pages and pages of tedium with Mr. ManWhore and Little Ms. Perfect, to get to the end. Overall, just a bloody awful book with not one redeeming quality.<br />My profound apologies to my buddy Amanda for making her read this with me! Not sure she’ll ever forgive me for this one… :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1464521189024542849" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer563843015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5452338376437575984">True Love Story is exactly what it is. A girl meets a boy, they fall in love, go through good times and not so good times, heartbreaking times, some sad and some happy moments, but in the end, true love endures and they live happily ever after. It’s the ultimate and amazing and breathtaking love story. And that whatever happens, if two people are meant to be together, nothing will keep them apart.<br/><blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413790ra/815125.gif' alt=' photo beautiful-couple-cute-love-love-story-Favimcom-292406_zpse265ce04.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote><br/>I loved Sparrow and Ian and liked seeing their relationship develop over a long period….</span>
  <span id="freeText5452338376437575984" style="display:none">True Love Story is exactly what it is. A girl meets a boy, they fall in love, go through good times and not so good times, heartbreaking times, some sad and some happy moments, but in the end, true love endures and they live happily ever after. It’s the ultimate and amazing and breathtaking love story. And that whatever happens, if two people are meant to be together, nothing will keep them apart.<br><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413790ra/815125.gif" alt=" photo beautiful-couple-cute-love-love-story-Favimcom-292406_zpse265ce04.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote><br>I loved Sparrow and Ian and liked seeing their relationship develop over a long period…..you experienced their journey with them.<br>I love this author's writing....<br><blockquote>
  <b>“You are in me. In the deepest part of me. Deeper than my memories, my unconscious thoughts. Deeper than my ever-changing emotions. You are in the place right next to where I keep my faith in God (a faith that I won't let go of now, in spite of it being shaken many times, from without and within). You're deep in me.” <br><br>“My life didn't begin until you breathed into it. ~ Ian” <br><br>“I suppose I might never have known or believed that love could be so strong if I hadn't seen it dragged through this hell. Now I know that love can truly endure anything.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>A very heart-wrenching, emotional and very beautifully written story.</span>

<div id="review_540561517" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/540561517" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/540561517?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=angst-filled-reads">angst-filled-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=rock-star-hero">rock-star-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=virginal-heroine">virginal-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer540561517" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13226615167296839962"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410335i/804433._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410335i/804434._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Gosh, this is a difficult one. I want to pretend that I am a realist and that I understand that love stories are not all sweetness and light, and I enjoy as much angst as the other one... but when I read a romance novel, I want to be completely and utterly in love with my hero.<br/><br/>And I was... that's part of the problem. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I can no more "go on" without you than I could if half my body was cut away.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I know this isn't making any sense, but bear with me. Ian Sterling is the <i>perfect</i> book boyfri</span>
  <span id="freeText13226615167296839962" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410335i/804433._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410335i/804434._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gosh, this is a difficult one. I want to pretend that I am a realist and that I understand that love stories are not all sweetness and light, and I enjoy as much angst as the other one... but when I read a romance novel, I want to be completely and utterly in love with my hero.<br><br>And I was... that's part of the problem. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I can no more "go on" without you than I could if half my body was cut away.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I know this isn't making any sense, but bear with me. Ian Sterling is the <i>perfect</i> book boyfriend. He's gorgeous, he's brazenly infatuated with our heroine, Sparrow. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"God, you're hot," he says. "I don't forget when we're apart - at all - but it just sort of shocks me all over again when I see you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>He's a sexy musician, he's got a tortured past and he does the cutest things... I'm talking cupcakes, writing songs about her, romantic getaways... I could go on. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Your boyfriend doesn't seem very attentive," he whispers.<br>"Oh, he's attentive," I whisper back.<br>"Well, I guess if you like them like that."<br>"Don't you worry about what I like."<br>"Can't promise you that."<br>"Why not?"<br>"Well, look at you. I already want to steal you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And that was where the problem lies...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're impossible." <br>"You're delectable."<br>"You're incorrigible."<br>"You're edible."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book broke my heart so badly that I'm not sure there was any chance of it ever being put back together again by the end of the book. I don't really know that Ian could possibly have redeemed himself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410335i/804435.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I assume that this is entitled <i>True Love Story</i>, with the emphasis on <i>True</i>, because of the ugliness in the book... the story is about truth, forgiveness, betrayal and ultimately a love that conquers all... but I'm not sure whether I believed or not. I don't know that I could have been as big a person as Sparrow was...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Love is enough.<br>Love does conquer all.<br>Love really does always protect, trust, hope, persevere...<br>I'd even go as far as saying that love never fails. I finally believe that. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Without spoilers, I can't really explain any further. I so did not see the twist coming. I don't know why because now that I know, it seems obvious... but anyhow, I didn't... and it knocked me for six.<br><br>All of that said. I could not put this book down. I loved reading it. Sparrow is fabulous. Sparrow and Ian's relationship, whilst a little unconventional, is addictive and, well... we've already discussed Ian.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>What's the right thing to do here? Is this a time when it really is okay to ogle? Or try to focus on his eyes in a loving way? I can't help it, I have to peek.<br>And that's what a real man looks like.<br>I had no idea it would be that... impressive.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Although I do have something to add... Anyone that can do a Justin Timberlake 'Damn Girl' strip tease and make it sexy needs to promoted to superhero in my book. I love love love this scene SO much!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I feel loved and pretty until I stump my toe on the floor. It wrecks my nail polish.<br>"Dang!"<br>Ian checks on my toe and then stands up and starts dancing seductively in front of me. He pulls off his t-shirt and starts singing in a high falsetto voice, "Dang girl, dang girl, dang girl, dang girl, dang girl, dang." He turns around and starts slowly pulling off his pajama bottoms, throwing in a pelvic thrust. "Dang girl, dang girl, dang girl, dang girl, dang girl, dang."<br>At first I'm staring wide-eyed at him and then I lose it. He runs his hand through his hair and goes for his underwear, ripping them off and my mouth drops before I die.<br>"You've got me saying, 'Dang girl, you're so fine. The way you let me put it down girl, just blows my mind. I guess I gotta put it down to-day. I gotta put it down..." he sings.<br>He's picked me up and it 'putting me down' on the bed. I'm wiping my eyes and trying to catch my breath. finally he stops and looks at me, grinning. "Dang girl, dang girl, dang..." he whispers as he kisses down my chest.<br>"You just put Justin Timberlake to shame," I tell him.<br>"Thanks, you inspired me with your 'dang'."<br>"I see that."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>So, I was so conflicted over how to rate this. As far as the writing and 90% of the book, it was a five star read... The characters were fantastic, it had me laughing out loud and I couldn't put it down...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I had to nip it in the butt," she says.<br>"Bud."<br>"What?"<br>"The bud. Nip it in the bud."<br>"I like the other way better."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>...but I just couldn't give it a perfect rating when it left me so torn. I <i>would</i> recommend this book, but I would advise going into it with an open mind. And I think that's about as much as I am able to say. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410335i/804436._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smittens-Book-Blog/525405204177978">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smitten...</a></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_485083179" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/485083179" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/485083179?book_show_action=true">Dec 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485083179" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17304254178998740957">Just from the <i>title</i> I knew this would be my kind of book and I wasn't wrong! So be prepared, this book is very angsty and emotional and such a wonderful love story. <br/><br/>It starts out in the present, with Sparrow running into her ex-boyfriend, Ian, who she hasn't seen in over a year....<i>a year, two months, and seventeen days</i> to be exact. Ian was very bad and Sparrow just couldn't forgive him but Ian tried so hard to make things better and he's never gotten over her. <br/><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786925i/489250._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/>We then get swept into the past t</span>
  <span id="freeText17304254178998740957" style="display:none">Just from the <i>title</i> I knew this would be my kind of book and I wasn't wrong! So be prepared, this book is very angsty and emotional and such a wonderful love story. <br><br>It starts out in the present, with Sparrow running into her ex-boyfriend, Ian, who she hasn't seen in over a year....<i>a year, two months, and seventeen days</i> to be exact. Ian was very bad and Sparrow just couldn't forgive him but Ian tried so hard to make things better and he's never gotten over her. <br><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786925i/489250._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>We then get swept into the past to when Sparrow and Ian met and I have to tell you that it's such a sweet and wonderful l♥ve story...I could not put the book down and I LOVED every moment of it. That is...until the drama happens and it is literally heartbreaking. But it hurts sooo good! <br><br>Ian, Ian, Ian...the thing you have to understand is that he is about nine years older than Sparrow and he's been around. He's not looking for anything serious and he's a musician going from city to city. That's scary enough but Sparrow doesn't care. I copied this picture from WA's facebook...he is the perfect Ian:<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786925i/489248._SX540_.jpg" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>When Sparrow and Ian meet, they just ~connect~ ...there's no other way to explain it except this is what you imagine soul mates to be. Of course, Sparrow knew who he was since he is a musician but being with him in person took things to a whole other level. They spend a wonderful day together but then Ian is distant. Come to find out he's told about the age difference and he doesn't want to ruin things for her. <br><br>Sparrow can't get him out of her mind and wants to be with him however she can get him and this is where all the warning signs start especially when they decide to be a couple Why would you not discuss being monogamous?? She's been warned, she's seen things for herself but she's too wrapped up in Ian to be objective. <br><br>The times when Ian and Sparrow are together are sooo lovely...it even made me a bit wistful but at times it was a bit much. Of course, when the drama that I've alluded to hits, Ian is really over the top. I do really love the letters but I needed more of an explanation and even though it seemed that Sparrow finally got it, we didn't and I feel cheated! It's a load of "crack"!! <br><br>And there's a bunch of other drama too. Things with family, with exes, with wannabes and with friends but nothing hurts like their time apart. "Agony. Torture. Anguish. Torment." Thank goodness for Tessa, Sparrow's best friend. When the story finally catches back up with the present, Sparrow has to decide on that age old question...Can she forgive? <br><br>There's sooo many sweet little gestures and things in the story that I would be remiss for not mentioning them. I loved the way Ian calls her "Little Bird", the "raw bows", the guitar picks, the elephant socks, the charm bracelet, the "librarian", the cupcakes and the houseboat.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786925i/489249.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There's a short but sweet epilogue and I loved how things ended up. It's a hard journey but a great love story and you won't regret taking the plunge. ♥ <br><br><br>Favorite quotes: <br><br>♥ “What are you doing to me, Sparrow Fisher?”<br><br>♥ "I've never been at home anywhere, but I am with you."<br><br>♥ "To be known. To be loved." <br><br>♥ “If you were looking for a sign from heaven, baby, I’d say they’re all around you. Take note.”<br><br>♥ “Aren’t you worn out from running?” His lips follow a tear down my neck, and then he brushes my face with his hand. “I don’t want to live without you <i>another day.</i> I’m begging you for another chance. <i>Please</i>.”<br><br>♥ “Ianow Orvillate Sterling,”</span>
  <a data-text-id="17304254178998740957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_515324722" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/515324722" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/515324722?book_show_action=true">Jan 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=male-groveling">male-groveling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-player">lead-character-player</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-s-famous">lead-character-s-famous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=first-love-crush">first-love-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-rockstar">lead-character-rockstar</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515324722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11435998518454615254">4.75 Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>W.B.T.<br/><br/>I suppose I might never have known or believed that love could be so strong if I hadn’t seen it dragged through this hell. Now I know that love can truly endure anything.</i>
</b><br/><br/>You know that feeling of finally finding a book that consumes you? That brings you out of that <i>book funk</i>? And when it ends, you’re in a haze. Not only because the story is over, but you’re sad that the journey you took has reached completion and now you’re back to that pesky ole <i>book funk</i>? Yep. That’s me righ</span>
  <span id="freeText11435998518454615254" style="display:none">4.75 Stars<br><br><b>
  <i>W.B.T.<br><br>I suppose I might never have known or believed that love could be so strong if I hadn’t seen it dragged through this hell. Now I know that love can truly endure anything.</i>
</b><br><br>You know that feeling of finally finding a book that consumes you? That brings you out of that <i>book funk</i>? And when it ends, you’re in a haze. Not only because the story is over, but you’re sad that the journey you took has reached completion and now you’re back to that pesky ole <i>book funk</i>? Yep. That’s me right here, right now. I’m in a sort of daze at the moment, but I feel compelled to write this review now because I know I just couldn’t wait to spread the word on how much I loved this story. I will warn you right now though: The <s>Love</s> story between Sparrow and Ian is not a pretty one. There were times where I was smiling and laughing one minute, then angry and extremely hurt the next. It was emotional, raw and just flat out addictive. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You have this grounding quality about you. I don’t know a better way to put it. It levels me. I’ve never been at home anywhere, but I am with you.” ~ Ian </i>
</b><br><br>The story begins with Sparrow and Ian cosmically meeting, again. They have met before, several times to be exact, but this meeting was different. We instantly find out that Ian broke Sparrow’s heart, but how? <br><br>Sparrow first met Ian when she was only eighteen years old. Even though she was already in a relationship at the time, the first time she meets Ian, she knew her life would never be the same. The connection they have is instantaneous. At this point in her life, Sparrow is just about to graduate and move to New York with her best friend, Tessa, to start college. Lots of changes are happening to Sparrow and throwing Ian into the mixture just made things a whole lot more interesting. <br><br><b>
  <i>“But seeing you, being near you, talking to you, hearing your laugh, watching your lips move, all of it. I felt awake. Alive. Crazed, almost. And I haven’t known what to do with it. Seeing you each time, it just intensifies, which never happens for me. With you, I just want more – instead of wanting to run, I want <u>more"</u> ~ Ian </i>
</b><br><br>Ian is a famous guitarist and songwriter. Through a series of events, Sparrow and Ian find themselves together at random times. Family gatherings, ski trips…they constantly run into each other; never really planning on running into each other. But when given the opportunity to be together, they take it. Ian isn’t really the “relationship” type, but he knows what he has with Sparrow is something special and he does not want to lose what he finds in her. She knows that they’ll be apart a lot, but they both decide to start a relationship, without really officially forming one. Don’t worry, it’ll all make sense once you read this. When Ian and Sparrow are together, they really <u>are</u> together. There is no doubt that these two are in love. The intensity of their relationship slowly grows with every encounter, but the talk of committing was never really fully discussed. Where is their relationship headed?<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m not a good person, Sparrow. I…I’m not. I look at you and I see all the good and I know that I could never deserve someone like you.” ~ Ian</i>
</b><br><br>Reading this story through Sparrow’s eyes, you felt everything that she felt. When Ian broke her heart, my heart broke as well. We both fell hard for him. I was so angry with some of the things he did; I didn’t think he was redeemable. However, there was always a flicker of light that kept on shining no matter how dark the times were. Ian is a broken man, I understood that. As for Sparrow, she <u>knew</u> what she was getting herself into. You prayed for a smooth road, but deep down you knew something was going to happen. Sorry if that’s spoilish, but every story has drama, and this one was no exception. <br><br>I loved this story, I really do. It wasn’t a perfect five start read, but it was close. This story will make you smile and Ian will make you melt. However, you will get angry and you will hurt when you read this. I think that’s why I loved it so much. Putting my heart in a blender does have it’s perks…you feel alive, <i>Crazed, almost</i> and I do admire that in a story. <br><br>-----<br><b>
  <u>FOLLOW ME</u>
</b><br><a href="http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/Banner2_zps7a6c719e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer2769473596312158069">5 Soul Wrenching stars!!<br/>I am a masochist for Epic Love stories like these!<br/><br/>******* This review WILL contain SPOILERS*******<br/><br/>The first time Sparrow sees Ian, it's practically Love at first sight...<br/>I really believe that love at first sight is true.. And this couple proves the theory...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798860.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ian and Sparrow are like magnets to each other, despite their age difference. But age really is a number when it comes to love...and their love story is epic and heartbreaking at the same time..<br/><br/><b>“You’re going to break m</b></span>
  <span id="freeText2769473596312158069" style="display:none">5 Soul Wrenching stars!!<br>I am a masochist for Epic Love stories like these!<br><br>******* This review WILL contain SPOILERS*******<br><br>The first time Sparrow sees Ian, it's practically Love at first sight...<br>I really believe that love at first sight is true.. And this couple proves the theory...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798860.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ian and Sparrow are like magnets to each other, despite their age difference. But age really is a number when it comes to love...and their love story is epic and heartbreaking at the same time..<br><br><b>“You’re going to break my heart, Sparrow Fisher.” And I think, Not before you break mine.” </b><br><br>When Ian and Sparrow can't ignore their feelings for each other, they start to date... At first Ian makes me crazy angry! Meeting Sparrow and being smitten by her then going for months without contacting her! NOT COOL!<br>Then she tells him that's she can't do this and they agree to date exclusively :D YAY!!!<br><br>Sparrow and Ian live in different cities due to Sparrow studying at NYU and Ian being a musician. They spend as much time together as they can and call and text... If you truely want something to work you will find a way to make it work. <br>Hey look at me, the ultimate romantic!! LoL!<br><br>They are sooo in love.. Crazy love some might call it.. I think it's truely special that they know what each other is thinking without even saying the words... <br><br>After a few months, Sparrow is head over heels in love with Ian and he in her...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798861.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me add that I didn't read any reviews before reading this because I didn't want to spoil it.<br>I was as HEAD OVER HEELS in love with Ian as Sparrow was...<br><br>He proposes!!! *SWOOOOON* and YES I'm more in love!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798862.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A few months before their wedding... <br>as expected, all good things come to an end.. It's like the universe is saying.. Hey you're happy, let me find a way to f*** it up. <br>Okay fine... Ian caused this on himself, he cheated on Sparrow for months in their relationship. She believes their relationship was a lie.. <br>When thinking about her feelings, a song came to mind...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798863.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> It BROKE my heart! HE broke my heart. I had a lump in my throat. I screamed texted... Cried texted...Yes u know who you are. Thanks for listening to my ranting :) <br><br>I totally understand why Sparrow cut him out of her life, I do... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798864.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's what he does afterwards that makes me WANT to forgive him!!<br>For months and months he writes her a letter everyday saying how sorry he is.. Sorry for what he did to her, to them, to their love... He prays for forgiveness, begs her for forgiveness... <br><br>She cannot let go.. But I FORGAVE HIM!!!!!! I'm SORRY but I just DO!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798865.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sparrow tells Ian that he needs to let go, she can't be with him...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798866._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Days, which turn into months, which turn into years ago by. Sparrow is still miserable. No one can make her feel the way Ian does. She dates other people and he does too but those are relationships doomed to failure.. How can you love someone when you already in love with someone else?<br><br>I strongly believe in the below..<br>1) You live once..<br>2) You love once..<br><br>And 2 years and ten months later when Sparrow is on a plane to her best friends wedding, Ian happens to be seated next to her... Fate has come back for them.<br><br><b>“If you were looking for a sign from heaven, baby, I’d say they’re all around you. Take note."</b><br><br>Finally Sparrow realizes that the only man that's going to make her happy is Ian.. <br><br><b>“Aren’t you worn out from running?” His lips follow a tear down my neck, and then he brushes my face with his hand. “I don’t want to live without you another day. I’m begging you for another chance. Please.” </b><br><br>She gives him another chance... Lets face it a love like this is one in a million..<br><br><b>“Love is enough.<br>Love does conquer all.<br>Love really does always protect, trust, hope, persevere...<br>I'd even go as far as saying that love never fails. I finally believe that.” </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408386i/798867.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They get married and Sparrow is pregnant!!! YAY!!!!! <br>Loved this story! Well done to the author!<br><br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer485046333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1265775752298315478"><b>5+++++++++++ Stars. This book was brilliant. I loved it. It was heartbreaking but in the end I got my hea and I couldn't be more delighted. This book lived up to be everything I had hoped and didn't let me down. A must read.</b></span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/484568139?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=made-me-feel">made-me-feel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=rockstar-love">rockstar-love</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer484568139" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15711662979538578861"> <b>FIVE + WE BELONG TOGETHER ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><b>Wow!</b> This book grabbed me from the opening scene and took me on a roller coaster ride of emotions, which is a favorite high for me. <br/><blockquote>
  <b>“Technically, he began breaking my heart the moment I met him, five years, eleven months, and one day ago.”</b>
</blockquote><br/>With that quote, I knew I was in for something good-bad-happy-sad-love-hate type of book. What I was not prepared for and delighted to experience was this well-written story with unique characters, from the MC’s to the second</span>
  <span id="freeText15711662979538578861" style="display:none"> <b>FIVE + WE BELONG TOGETHER ★★★★★</b><br /><br /><b>Wow!</b> This book grabbed me from the opening scene and took me on a roller coaster ride of emotions, which is a favorite high for me. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>“Technically, he began breaking my heart the moment I met him, five years, eleven months, and one day ago.”</b>
</blockquote><br />With that quote, I knew I was in for something good-bad-happy-sad-love-hate type of book. What I was not prepared for and delighted to experience was this well-written story with unique characters, from the MC’s to the secondary that I absolutely feel in book love with. Sparrow, our heroine has become a favorite of mine. I adored her sense of humor, her relationship with her parents, her life choices, her struggles and her cuss/non cuss words. Ian, our hero or anti-hero as some may call him, is beautifully perfect and not. My heart broke right along with Sparrow’s but it was also mended again, and full of love for Ian. Sure I was livid over some of his choices but I accepted them, understood them and moved on with a lump in my throat over the ‘Letters’ Ohh… boo hoo… I was slayed and could only wish that Sparrow would see what I did. <br /><br />I know I am sounding like a crazy fan-girl, but I loved this ‘True Love Story’ and I would hope other readers get to feel what I feel from reading this book. I am definitely in book hangover mode from this one so much so that I will be doing a reread right away and then give this book a proper review…<br /><br />For now, I am going to leave just a sample of my favorite quotes:<br /><br /><b>“The guys are calling me Red Raw. Red Raw Bows, to be exact.” “Ha, Red Raw Bows? Why?” “My elbows are bright red, like carpet burn … raw”</b><br /><br /><b>“If there were a line-up of a thousand penises, I’d recognize his in a heartbeat”</b><br /><br /><b>“Little Bird, our love has been hard-earned from the very beginning. It is more precious to me than anything on earth. I can’t just let go of it. And I won’t stop fighting for it”</b><br /><br /> <b>“I still believe in us, Sparrow. I’ll never stop”</b><br /> <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15711662979538578861" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_541638680" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/541638680" />
    <a title="Marina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13500406-marina"><img alt="Marina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1361224250p2/13500406.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/541638680?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marina" href="/user/show/13500406-marina">Marina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=delicious-bad-boys">delicious-bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=in-one-word-good">in-one-word-good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13500406-marina?shelf=food-for-thought">food-for-thought</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer541638680" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13140227166458264481"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I cry for everything that’s lost. I cry that he gave up. I cry for the anger in his words. I cry that he’s found someone that has made him consider letting me go. I cry for the day I ever met him and thought I could handle someone like him. I cry that the girl he met that day in the restaurant is long gone.<br/>And I cry because I don’t know what to do with this person that’s left.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/>I usually start a review with the quote that somehow gives the gist, the general feeling, a small snippet on </span>
  <span id="freeText13140227166458264481" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I cry for everything that’s lost. I cry that he gave up. I cry for the anger in his words. I cry that he’s found someone that has made him consider letting me go. I cry for the day I ever met him and thought I could handle someone like him. I cry that the girl he met that day in the restaurant is long gone.<br>And I cry because I don’t know what to do with this person that’s left.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>I usually start a review with the quote that somehow gives the gist, the general feeling, a small snippet on the powerful love story, if it is such a one. But I think that this confession is worth placing it on the top. Because a book that puts you in the shoes of the person who suffers, is certainly worth mentioning. Of both their pains.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410500i/804993.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>Ian.</b><br>It's curious what happens when you know from the beginning that something emotionally hellish is going to come down. And you also know it's his fault. And further than that you are given a vague idea of what that is.<br><br>And yet, you can see that he is not an as*hole. Meaning that he's not an obnoxiously cocky alpha bastard who screws up royally, intentionally.<br><br>I can believe that.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Sparrow,” his voice comes out in a husky rasp, “you couldn’t possibly be any more gorgeous. You …” he shakes his head and pulls on his lips in that nervous gesture that always gave him away. “God, you make my insides shake.” He laughs and then he realizes he has an audience. <br>“Sorry, that was probably way more than any of you needed to know.” He looks at Jared and Tessa who are staring at him with slack jaws. “Sparrow here turned me into a “feely man” when she exposed my dark side. I used to be so stoic and mysterious, and now I spew things like ‘God, you make my insides shake.’” Ian looks around and laughs awkwardly and now my jaw is hanging open too.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br>That doesn't stop you from thinking:<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410500i/804994.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><br>At some point the book mentions that <i>Love conquers all</i>.<br>I don't believe that.<br>But I do believe that if people will it, they can conquer all. That it all comes down to sheer will.<br>Because let's face it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410500i/804995.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>Sparrow.</b><br>The girl is lovely. Just purely lovely. And also tears you apart.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I do believe he loves me.<br>I just don’t believe it’s enough.<br>I wasn’t enough for him for the last couple of years, why would I think I could be enough now?</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410500i/804996.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>“Why?” It gushes out, sounding foreign through all the tears. “Why, Ian? What did she have that I didn’t? Why wasn’t I enough? How could you take<br>my feelings and just toss them aside like trash? I lived for you.” I’m choking now and making horrific, gasping sounds, but I can’t stop. “I believed<br>you loved me. I trusted you. I thought what we had was beyond any love I’d ever seen. Why did you throw it away? Again and again?”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410500i/804997.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><br>And still you can't help feeling happy when people, even fictional ones, find the way to sort things out. To sort themselves out.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He lifts the top of the box and stares. Nestled in pretty tissue paper, so he doesn’t have to touch it, I have the pregnancy test laying face up.<br>That plus sign might as well be blinking for how vivid it looks against the tissue.<br>Ian sets the box down and I look up to see his reaction. He looks stunned, and then he’s laughing and has tears running down his face at the same time. He grasps my face in both hands, kissing me hard. Then he kisses his way down to my stomach.<br>“Ianow Orvillate Sterling,” he whispers, grinning up at me, “you were made with love.”</b>
  </i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410500i/804998.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <br>
  <i>
    <b>You are my first<br>And last<br>And only<br>True Love—<br>Ian</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13140227166458264481" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer541305523" class="readable"
